Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direccin del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |uniform vec3 spherePos;
 18 |uniform float sphereSize;
 19 |
 20 |layout (triangles) in;
 21 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 22 |
 23 |in vec4 color[3];
 24 |out vec4 fragColor;
 25 |
 26 |vec3 faceCenter, b1, b2, pointWorld;
 27 |bool t, j, b;
 28 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 29 |
 30 |void main() {
 31 |	faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis * cylinderHeight;
 32 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 33 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 34 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0;
 35 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 36 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) 
 37 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos)) <= cylinderRadius;
 38 |
 39 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 40 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 41 |		}
 42 |	}
 43 |
 44 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 45 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 46 |		fragColor = color[i];
 47 |
 48 |		switch (verticesInsideCylinder) {
 49 |			case 0:
 50 |				EmitVertex();
 51 |				break;
 52 |			case 1:
 53 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 54 |				EmitVertex();
 55 |				break;
 56 |			case 2:
 57 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 58 |				EmitVertex()
 59 |				break;
 60 |		}
 61 |		EndPrimitive();
 62 |	}
 63 |}

 26 |vec3 faceCenter, b1, b2, pointWorld;
 27 |bool t, j, b;
 28 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 29 |
 30 |void main() {
 31 |	faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis * cylinderHeight;
 32 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 33 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 34 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0;
 35 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 36 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) 
 37 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos)) <= cylinderRadius;
 38 |
 39 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 40 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 41 |		}
 42 |	}
 43 |
 44 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 45 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 46 |		fragColor = color[i];
 47 |
 48 |		switch (verticesInsideCylinder) {
 49 |			case 0:
 50 |				EmitVertex();
 51 |				break;
 52 |			case 1:
 53 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 54 |				EmitVertex();
 55 |				break;
 56 |			case 2:
 57 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 58 |				EmitVertex()
 59 |				break;
 60 |		}
 61 |		EndPrimitive();
 62 |	}
 63 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direccin del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |uniform vec3 spherePos;
 18 |uniform float sphereSize;
 19 |
 20 |layout (triangles) in;
 21 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 22 |
 23 |in vec4 color[3];
 24 |out vec4 fragColor;
 25 |
 26 |vec3 faceCenter, b1, b2, pointWorld;
 27 |bool t, j, b;
 28 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 29 |
 30 |void main() {
 31 |	faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis * cylinderHeight;
 32 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 33 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 34 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 35 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 36 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) 
 37 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos)) <= cylinderRadius;
 38 |
 39 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 40 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 41 |		}
 42 |	}
 43 |
 44 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 45 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 46 |		fragColor = color[i];
 47 |
 48 |		switch (verticesInsideCylinder) {
 49 |			case 0:
 50 |				EmitVertex();
 51 |				break;
 52 |			case 1:
 53 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 54 |				EmitVertex();
 55 |				break;
 56 |			case 2:
 57 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 58 |				EmitVertex()
 59 |				break;
 60 |		}
 61 |		EndPrimitive();
 62 |	}
 63 |}

 46 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 47 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 48 |		fragColor = color[i];
 49 |
 50 |		switch (verticesInsideCylinder) {
 51 |			case 0:
 52 |				EmitVertex();
 53 |				break;
 54 |			case 1:
 55 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 56 |				EmitVertex();
 57 |				break;
 58 |			case 2:
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |				EmitVertex();
 61 |				break;
 62 |		}
 63 |		EndPrimitive();
 64 |	}
 65 |}

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |in vec3 position;
 13 |in vec3 normal;
 14 |
 15 |
 16 |// Posicin de la fuente en el espacio de la cmara
 17 |uniform vec3 lightpos;
 18 |// Color difuso del objeto
 19 |uniform vec4 diffuseColor;
 20 |
 21 |out vec4 color;
 22 |
 23 |void main() {
 24 |	// Normal en el espacio de la cmara
 25 |	vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix *normal);
 26 |	// Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
 27 |	vec4 pos4 = vec4(position, 1.0);
 28 |	vec3 eposition=vec3(modelviewMatrix * pos4);
 29 |	// Clculo de la iluminacin
 30 |	color = max(0.0, dot(eN, normalize(lightpos-eposition))) * diffuseColor;
 31 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * pos4;
 32 |}
 33 |
Fragment shader: ../p6/p6.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |in vec4 color;
  4 |
  5 |out vec4 finalColor;
  6 |
  7 |
  8 |void main() {
  9 |	finalColor = color;	
 10 |}
Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direccin del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |uniform vec3 spherePos;
 18 |uniform float sphereSize;
 19 |
 20 |layout (triangles) in;
 21 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 22 |
 23 |in vec4 color[3];
 24 |out vec4 fragColor;
 25 |
 26 |vec3 faceCenter, b1, b2, pointWorld;
 27 |bool t, j, b;
 28 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 29 |
 30 |void main() {
 31 |	faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis * cylinderHeight;
 32 |
 33 |	verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 34 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 35 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 36 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 37 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 38 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) 
 39 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos)) <= cylinderRadius;
 40 |
 41 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 42 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 43 |		}
 44 |	}
 45 |
 46 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 47 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 48 |		fragColor = color[i];
 49 |
 50 |		switch (verticesInsideCylinder) {
 51 |			case 0:
 52 |				EmitVertex();
 53 |				break;
 54 |			case 1:
 55 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 56 |				EmitVertex();
 57 |				break;
 58 |			case 2:
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |				EmitVertex();
 61 |				break;
 62 |		}
 63 |		EndPrimitive();
 64 |	}
 65 |}

 26 |	// Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
 27 |	vec4 pos4 = vec4(position, 1.0);
 28 |	vec3 eposition=vec3(modelviewMatrix * pos4);
 29 |	// Clculo de la iluminacin
 30 |	color = max(0.0, dot(eN, normalize(lightpos-eposition))) * diffuseColor;
 31 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * pos4;
 32 |}
 33 |
Fragment shader: ../p6/p6.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |in vec4 color;
  4 |
  5 |out vec4 finalColor;
  6 |
  7 |
  8 |void main() {
  9 |	finalColor = color;	
 10 |}
Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direccin del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |uniform vec3 spherePos;
 18 |uniform float sphereSize;
 19 |
 20 |layout (triangles) in;
 21 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 22 |
 23 |in vec4 color[3];
 24 |out vec4 fragColor;
 25 |
 26 |vec3 faceCenter, b1, b2, pointWorld;
 27 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 28 |
 29 |void main() {
 30 |	faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis * cylinderHeight;
 31 |
 32 |	verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 33 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 34 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 35 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 36 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 37 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) 
 38 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos)) <= cylinderRadius;
 39 |
 40 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 41 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 42 |		}
 43 |	}
 44 |
 45 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 46 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 47 |		fragColor = color[i];
 48 |
 49 |		switch (verticesInsideCylinder) {
 50 |			case 0:
 51 |				EmitVertex();
 52 |				break;
 53 |			case 1:
 54 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 55 |				EmitVertex();
 56 |				break;
 57 |			case 2:
 58 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 59 |				EmitVertex();
 60 |				break;
 61 |		}
 62 |		EndPrimitive();
 63 |	}
 64 |}

  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // Unit vector
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // Center of the base
 16 |
 17 |uniform vec3 spherePos;
 18 |uniform float sphereSize;
 19 |
 20 |layout (triangles) in;
 21 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 22 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 23 |
 24 |in vec4 color[3];
 25 |out vec4 fragColor;
 26 |
 27 |vec3 faceCenter, pointWorld;
 28 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 29 |
 30 |void main() {
 31 |	faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis * cylinderHeight;
 32 |
 33 |	verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 34 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 35 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 36 |		/*
 37 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 38 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 39 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) 
 40 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos)) <= cylinderRadius;
 41 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 42 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 43 |		}
 44 |								   */
 45 |		bool t = (dot((pointWorld-cylinderPos),(pointWorld-cylinderPos)) >= 0) && (dot((pointWorld-pointWorld),(cylinderPos-pointWorld)) >= 0);
 46 |		bool j = length(cross((pointWorld-cylinderPos),(pointWorld-cylinderPos)))/length(pointWorld-cylinderPos) <= r;
 47 |	}
 48 |
 49 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 50 |		gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 51 |		fragColor = color[i];
 52 |
 53 |		switch (verticesInsideCylinder) {
 54 |			case 0:
 55 |				EmitVertex();
 56 |				break;
 57 |			case 1:
 58 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 59 |				EmitVertex();
 60 |				break;
 61 |			case 2:
 62 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 63 |				EmitVertex();
 64 |				break;
 65 |		}
 66 |	}
 67 |	EndPrimitive();

  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // Unit vector
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // Center of the base
 16 |
 17 |uniform vec3 spherePos;
 18 |uniform float sphereSize;
 19 |
 20 |layout (triangles) in;
 21 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 22 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 23 |
 24 |in vec4 color[3];
 25 |out vec4 fragColor;
 26 |
 27 |vec3 faceCenter, pointWorld;
 28 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 29 |
 30 |void main() {
 31 |	faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis cylinderHeight;
 32 |
 33 |	verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 34 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 35 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 36 |		
 37 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 38 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 39 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) 
 40 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos)) <= cylinderRadius;
 41 |
 42 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 43 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 44 |		}
 45 |	}
 46 |
 47 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 48 |		gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 49 |		fragColor = color[i];
 50 |
 51 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 52 |			EmitVertex();
 53 |		}
 54 |		else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 55 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 56 |			EmitVertex();
 57 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 58 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 59 |			EmitVertex();
 60 |		}
 61 |		EmitVertex();
 62 |	}
 63 |	EndPrimitive();
 64 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // Unit vector
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // Center of the base
 16 |
 17 |uniform vec3 spherePos;
 18 |uniform float sphereSize;
 19 |
 20 |layout (triangles) in;
 21 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 22 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 23 |
 24 |in vec4 color[3];
 25 |out vec4 fragColor;
 26 |
 27 |vec3 faceCenter, pointWorld;
 28 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 29 |
 30 |void main() {
 31 |	faceCenter =  projMatrix * viewMatrix *cylinderPos +  projMatrix * viewMatrix *cylinderAxis *  projMatrix * viewMatrix *cylinderHeight;
 32 |
 33 |	verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 34 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 35 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 36 |		
 37 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 38 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 39 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos)) 
 40 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos) <= cylinderRadius;
 41 |
 42 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 43 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 44 |		}
 45 |	}
 46 |
 47 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 48 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 49 |		fragColor = color[i];
 50 |
 51 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 52 |			EmitVertex();
 53 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 54 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 55 |			EmitVertex();
 56 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 57 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 58 |			EmitVertex();
 59 |		}
 60 |	}
 61 |	EndPrimitive();
 62 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // Unit vector
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // Center of the base
 16 |
 17 |uniform vec3 spherePos;
 18 |uniform float sphereSize;
 19 |
 20 |layout (triangles) in;
 21 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 22 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 23 |
 24 |in vec4 color[3];
 25 |out vec4 fragColor;
 26 |
 27 |vec3 faceCenter, pointWorld;
 28 |int verticesInsideCylinder;
 29 |
 30 |void main() {
 31 |	faceCenter =  projMatrix * viewMatrix *cylinderPos +  projMatrix * viewMatrix *cylinderAxis *  projMatrix * viewMatrix *cylinderHeight;
 32 |
 33 |	verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 34 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 35 |		pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 36 |		
 37 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 38 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 39 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos)) 
 40 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos) <= cylinderRadius;
 41 |
 42 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 43 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 44 |		}
 45 |	}
 46 |
 47 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 48 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 49 |		fragColor = color[i];
 50 |
 51 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 52 |			EmitVertex();
 53 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 54 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 55 |			EmitVertex();
 56 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 57 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 58 |			EmitVertex();
 59 |		}
 60 |	}
 61 |	EndPrimitive();
 62 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis;
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos;
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	vec3 faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis * cylinderHeight;
 26 |
 27 |	vec3 faceCenter = vec4(cylinderPos, 1.0);
 28 |
 29 |	int verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 30 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 31 |		vec3 pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 32 |		
 33 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 34 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 35 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos)) 
 36 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos) <= cylinderRadius;
 37 |
 38 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 39 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 40 |		}
 41 |	}
 42 |
 43 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 44 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 45 |		fragColor = color[i];
 46 |
 47 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 48 |			EmitVertex();
 49 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 50 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 51 |			EmitVertex();
 52 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 53 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 54 |			EmitVertex();
 55 |		}
 56 |	}
 57 |	EndPrimitive();
 58 |}

 51 |			EmitVertex();
 52 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 53 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 54 |			EmitVertex();
 55 |		}
 56 |	}
 57 |	EndPrimitive();
 58 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis;
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos;
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	//vec3 faceCenter = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis * cylinderHeight;
 26 |
 27 |	vec3 faceCenter = vec4(cylinderPos.x, cylinderPos.y, cylinderPos.z, 1.0);
 28 |
 29 |	int verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 30 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 31 |		vec3 pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 32 |		
 33 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 34 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 35 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos)) 
 36 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos) <= cylinderRadius;
 37 |
 38 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 39 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 40 |		}
 41 |	}
 42 |
 43 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 44 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 45 |		fragColor = color[i];
 46 |
 47 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 48 |			EmitVertex();
 49 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 50 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 51 |			EmitVertex();
 52 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 53 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 54 |			EmitVertex();
 55 |		}
 56 |	}
 57 |	EndPrimitive();
 58 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis;
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos;
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	vec3 bottomFaceCenter = (viewMatrix * vec4(cylinderPos.x, cylinderPos.y, cylinderPos.z, 1.0)).xyz;
 26 |	vec3 topFaceCenter = (bottomFaceCenter + cylinderPos * (viewMatrix * vec4(cylinderAxis, 1.0)));
 27 |
 28 |	int verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 29 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 30 |		vec3 pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 31 |		
 32 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 33 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 34 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos)) 
 35 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos) <= cylinderRadius;
 36 |
 37 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 38 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 39 |		}
 40 |	}
 41 |
 42 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 43 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 44 |		fragColor = color[i];
 45 |
 46 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 47 |			EmitVertex();
 48 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 49 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 50 |			EmitVertex();
 51 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 52 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 53 |			EmitVertex();
 54 |		}
 55 |	}
 56 |	EndPrimitive();
 57 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis;
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos;
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	vec3 bottomFaceCenter = (viewMatrix * vec4(cylinderPos.x, cylinderPos.y, cylinderPos.z, 1.0)).xyz;
 26 |	vec3 topFaceCenter = (bottomFaceCenter + cylinderPos * (viewMatrix * vec4(cylinderAxis, 1.0)).xyz);
 27 |
 28 |	int verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 29 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 30 |		vec3 pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 31 |		
 32 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 33 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - faceCenter) >= 0.0;
 34 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, faceCenter - cylinderPos)) 
 35 |		                           / length(faceCenter - cylinderPos) <= cylinderRadius;
 36 |
 37 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 38 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 39 |		}
 40 |	}
 41 |
 42 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 43 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 44 |		fragColor = color[i];
 45 |
 46 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 47 |			EmitVertex();
 48 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 49 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 50 |			EmitVertex();
 51 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 52 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 53 |			EmitVertex();
 54 |		}
 55 |	}
 56 |	EndPrimitive();
 57 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/p6.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis;
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos;
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	vec3 bottomFaceCenter = (viewMatrix * vec4(cylinderPos.x, cylinderPos.y, cylinderPos.z, 1.0)).xyz;
 26 |	vec3 topFaceCenter = (bottomFaceCenter + (viewMatrix * vec4(cylinderAxis, 0.0)).xyz * cylinderHeight);
 27 |	
 28 |	int verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 29 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 30 |		vec3 pointWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 31 |		
 32 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(pointWorld - cylinderPos, bottomFaceCenter - cylinderPos) >= 0.0
 33 |		                         && dot(pointWorld - faceCenter, cylinderPos - topFaceCenter) >= 0.0;
 34 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(pointWorld - cylinderPos, bottomFaceCenter - cylinderPos)) 
 35 |		                           / length(topFaceCenter - cylinderPos) <= cylinderRadius;
 36 |
 37 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 38 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 39 |		}
 40 |	}
 41 |
 42 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 43 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * viewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 44 |		fragColor = color[i];
 45 |
 46 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 47 |			EmitVertex();
 48 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 49 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 50 |			EmitVertex();
 51 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 52 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 53 |			EmitVertex();
 54 |		}
 55 |	}
 56 |	EndPrimitive();
 57 |	
 58 |}

  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius;
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight;
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis;
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos;
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	vec3 bottomFaceCenter = (viewMatrix * vec4(cylinderPos.x, cylinderPos.y, cylinderPos.z, 1.0)).xyz;
 26 |	vec3 topFaceCenter = bottomFaceCenter + ((viewMatrix * vec4(cylinderAxis.x, cylinderAxis.y, cylinderAxis.z, 0.0)).xyz * cylinderHeight;
 27 |	
 28 |	int verticesInsideCylinder = 0;
 29 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 30 |		vec3 vertexPosWorld = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz;
 31 |		
 32 |		bool betweenCylinderFaces = dot(vertexPosWorld - bottomFaceCenter, topFaceCenter - bottomFaceCenter) >= 0.0
 33 |		                         && dot(vertexPosWorld - topFaceCenter, bottomFaceCenter - topFaceCenter) >= 0.0;
 34 |		bool insideCylinderSurface = length(cross(vertexPosWorld - bottomFaceCenter, topFaceCenter - bottomFaceCenter)) 
 35 |		                           / length(topFaceCenter - bottomFaceCenter) <= cylinderRadius;
 36 |
 37 |		if (betweenCylinderFaces && insideCylinderSurface) {
 38 |			++verticesInsideCylinder;
 39 |		}
 40 |	}
 41 |
 42 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); ++i) {
 43 |		gl_Position = projMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 44 |		fragColor = color[i];
 45 |
 46 |		if (verticesInsideCylinder == 0) {
 47 |			EmitVertex();
 48 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 1) {
 49 |			fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 50 |			EmitVertex();
 51 |		} else if (verticesInsideCylinder == 2) {
 52 |			fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 53 |			EmitVertex();
 54 |		}
 55 |	}
 56 |	EndPrimitive();
 57 |	
 58 |}
